The hotel service attitude is very good. Although the waiter in the elevator did not take the initiative to greet you, you can still feel that the hotel atmosphere is very good, which also saves customers from embarrassment sometimes. The floor is very high, the view is very good, and the elevator is very stable. However, during the stay, one of the elevators leaked. At first, the customer manager found it and blocked it with his body. But when the customer arrived, they still let him get on the elevator. I hope they will block the door with a yellow sign next time. When I got off the elevator and arrived at the floor where I stayed, the carpet was very nice. After entering the room, I found that the facilities were complete. I liked the chair at the door very much. The bathroom and bedroom were separated. The bed was very comfortable. The night light was well designed. It was just that the floor made a little noise when I walked on it. When I filled the toilet, the floor drain in the bathroom made a lot of noise. The toilet facilities were very complete (telephone, alarm, socket). There were many varieties of breakfast, but the taste was average. There was a gym, which was small but very complete. The swimming pool was very large. Due to family reasons, I canceled one night and the hotel agreed very happily. Overall, the hotel is worth recommending.

msg:If you come to Jinling, the ancient capital of the Six Dynasties, Golden Eagle International Hotel is the first choice. An old-fashioned high-end hotel located in the city center, with convenient transportation and very close to the subway station. If you only have a small amount of luggage, you can take the subway directly to Xinjiekou after getting off the high-speed rail, then walk and stroll in the underground passage, eat and drink directly to the exit outside the hotel lobby. If you have a little more luggage, if you take the subway, you can transfer to another subway line at Xinjiekou and get off at Shanghai Station. It takes only 5 minutes to walk to the hotel. Stepping into the hotel, you will be surrounded by a relaxing aroma. The lobby is dark, elegant and luxurious, and there are guests sitting in twos and threes talking softly on the sofa. The beautiful lady at the check-in front desk speaks softly and makes people feel very cordial. Although I arrived before noon and it was not check-in time, the young lady quickly checked me in and upgraded the room for free. As soon as I entered the room on the 45th floor, what awaited me was another surprise. The retro layout of the porch not only improves the privacy, but also adds to the charm of the room. The room is not only large, but also has a very high floor, a large space, not oppressive, and you can see Mochou Lake and Qinhuai River in the distance, and the night view is even more dazzling and charming, especially amazing. Sitting on the sofa in front of the floor-to-ceiling windows, drinking a cup of coffee and overlooking the sweeping city view outside the window is also an excellent enjoyment. The bedding is comfortable, the room is well soundproofed and very quiet. The toiletry set is L'Occitane, which is my favorite fragrance. Room service is on call and responsive to every request. Ms. Yang Qianqian at the front desk also gave me a note for late check-out. The price of the set meal I bought this time is cheaper than the listed price. It includes a box of the hotel's latest premium rice dumplings and salted duck eggs. The rice dumplings taste very good. Breakfast is not included in the package, but the Nanjing special soup dumplings, duck blood vermicelli, small wontons, brown sugar taro soup, etc. in the Jiming Tangbao shop opposite the hotel are all delicious. If you want to taste Nanjing delicacies, don‚Äôt miss it! Of course, there are also many snacks in the underground supermarket in front of the hotel. In short, although only stayed for one night, it left good memories. Next time I have the opportunity to come to Nanjing, I will choose Golden Eagle International.
